                  </form>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">تَبَعٌ</foreign> (S, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">تَبَاعَةٌ</foreign>, (S, K,) <hi rend="ital">He followed;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">went,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">walked, behind,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">after;</hi> (S, Mgh, Msb, K;) <hi rend="ital">him,</hi> (Mgh, Msb, K,) or <hi rend="ital">it;</hi> namely, a people, or company of men: (S:) or [in the CK “ and ”] <hi rend="ital">he went with him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, when the latter had passed by him:</hi> (S, Mgh, Msb, K:) and

      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n3724-4" target="أَتْبَعْتُهُ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> signify the same: and hence the saying in the Kur [xxxvii. 10], <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n3724-5" target="فَأَتْبَعَهُ" n="5" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>شِهَابٌ ثَاقِبٌ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">and a shooting star piercing the darkness by its light overtaketh him</hi>]: (S:) and the saying in the same [vii. 174],

      <foreign lang="ar">مَا زِلْتُ <ref cref="n3724-11" target="أَتَّبِعُهُمْ" n="11" type="5" subtype="FTO" lang="ar"/>حَتَّى </foreign>, i. e. [<hi rend="ital">I ceased not to follow them</hi>] <hi rend="ital">until I overtook them:</hi> (A'Obeyd:) Fr says that

(Mgh.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">تَبِعْتُ الرَّجُلَ بِحَقِّى</foreign>; and <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n3724-23" target="تَابَعْتُهُ" n="23" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>بِهِ</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">مُتَابَعَةٌ</foreign> [and probably <foreign lang="ar">تبَاعٌ</foreign> also]; and <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n3724-24" target="اِتَّبَعْتُهُ" n="24" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>به</foreign>; <hi rend="ital">I prosecuted,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">sued, the man for my right,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">due.</hi> (TA.)
